# Error numbers 5000 to 5999 are reserved for X Plugin. Please do not use

#
# Start of 8.0 error messages intended to be logged to the server error log.
#
# Note:
#     *) Error messages intended to be sent to client should *not* be added here.
#        Please add them to "8.0 error messages" section.
#
#     *) If the same error message is intended to be logged to the server
#        error log and also sent to the client, add separate error codes:
#        One for the server error log and another to send to the client.
#
start-error-number 10000
